Important News 2

Abducted German Missionaries in Meixian Have Been Rescued

Shantou Correspondence: Two years ago, German missionaries Wan Jinghe and He San, were abducted by Gu Dacun's communist bandits while summering at the highest peak of Qingliang Mountain, on the border of Meixian and Fengshun counties. The bandits demanded a huge ransom, and the church could not afford the enormous sum. The three missionaries also wrote to the church, asking them not to pay the ransom, but to pray more. They vowed to dedicate their lives to spreading the gospel and practicing medicine in China, believing that their abduction was divinely ordained and that they would be released. Later, the missionaries practiced medicine and did good deeds among the bandits, and this spring they were released unconditionally. This year, Commander Xiang has been extremely diligent in suppressing local communists in Fengshun County, destroying the bandit nests in the Eight Villages Mountains and Jiulongzhang. The remaining bandits have been nearly wiped out. Today, a telegram was received from Kong Kequan's regiment stationed in Fengshun, stating that Chen Kuiya and his wife, standing committee members of the East River Farmers' and Workers' Soldiers' Representative Council of the Communist Party, and over a hundred Red Guards were hiding in Shangyang, Qilangdangshi, and Jiulongzhang. The regiment dispatched the companies of Fu Changguang, Tan Yin, and Yang Guishan to search the bandit nests in Yingge Deli, Yangqian Pit, Shangyang, Qilangdangshi, and Gouwei Ji. In this operation, 13 bandits were killed, and the office of the Red Army Guard Corps was destroyed, seizing rifles, carbines, red flags, propaganda materials, etc. Chen Kuiya escaped. Furthermore, on the evening of the 10th, He Naiying, the Magistrate of Fengshun County, personally led a bandit suppression team to the Shijiaotang Stone Cave in Dashen Township and rescued the German missionaries He Yungong and Wan Baoquan, who had been abducted by bandits two years ago. They were sent back to the county office on the 11th. Although the two missionaries are old, they are fortunately healthy as ever. However, having lived in the mountains for a long time, they appear slightly pale and emaciated with shaggy beards and hair. They were sent back to Meixian during the day. (December 15th)

The Truth Behind the Situation on the Kang Border

War Between Daji Temple in Xikang and Bairi Tusi

Xikang Correspondence: The war between Daji Lamasery in Ganzi County, Xikang North Road, and Bairi Tusi over the reincarnation of the Living Buddha and inheritance issues has been going on for several months. Because both sides have backgrounds, the local war is gradually affecting the overall situation in Kang and Tibet. Although the Central Government has ordered a halt to the offensive, the war has not yet ended. The general situation of Daji Temple, its relationship with Tibet, and the process of the current war are described below for those who are concerned about border affairs.

Overview of Daji Temple: According to records, Daji Lamasery was initially only a third-class temple with only several hundred lamas. Since the end of the Qing Dynasty, there have been many border incidents and endless wars between Sichuan and Tibet. When the Sichuan army won, they advanced westward, and when the Tibetan army won, they invaded eastward. In this back-and-forth, the people of Kang were already unable to bear it, especially the wealthy lamasery. Regardless of whether the Han or Tibetan troops arrived, they would accuse them of colluding with the enemy, looting, and burning them at will. Therefore, the top first- and second-class temples have declined. Only Daji Temple in this area has been able to survive unscathed due to its ability to deal with the situation. More and more monks from all directions have returned to it. Moreover, because Ganzi is a wealthy area, the lamas of the temple use temple property to engage in business, and their capital has been increasing day by day, making them one of the wealthiest in the area, which has long been coveted by others. In the fifth year of the Republic of China, the people of Xiangcheng in Xikang South Road, coveting its wealth, gathered a cavalry of 1,000 men to besiege it for three days and nights, but were eventually repelled. Since then, the temple has expanded its military force to defend against foreign aggression. It is estimated that the temple has over 1,800 lamas, over 2,000 quick-firing rifles, and over 2,000 good horses. Outsiders are not allowed to enter the temple on weekdays, and the Ganzi magistrate can only deal with it perfunctorily.

Relationship with Tibet: Ganzi County is under the jurisdiction of the Commander-in-Chief of the Sichuan-Kang Border. More than a hundred li to the west is the garrison of the Tibetan army (note that the Tibetan army advanced to Ganzi after invading eastward in the sixth year of the Republic of China). The Dalai Lama, seeing the wealth and military strength of Daji Temple, and its location in the throat of Xikang North Road, deeply desired to use it as a base for eastward invasion. Therefore, he spared no effort to win it over and supplied it with money and guns. In the twelfth year of the Republic of China, when Chen Xialing, the Garrison Commander of the Sichuan Border, was defeated, Daji Temple disarmed the few Sichuan troops stationed in Ganzi, which was the result of the Dalai Lama's instigation. From then on, the Dalai Lama's desire to use Daji Temple became even more urgent, and he often sent special personnel to give gifts and rewards to the lamas. Moreover, all lamas from the temple who went to Tibet were treated favorably. Having received such special treatment, the temple naturally prostrated itself before the Dalai Lama.

The Process of the War: This war was caused by a conflict between Daji Temple and the local Bairi Tusi over the enthronement of a Living Buddha and inheritance issues (note that Bairi Tusi is one of the major Tusi in the North Road, and although Zhao Erfeng of the Qing Dynasty changed the system of Tusi and returned the land to the government, the local people still mostly believe in him). Initially, neighboring Tusi Baozheng mediated, and then the Ganzi County Magistrate came out to persuade them, but to no avail. Daji Temple relied on its strong manpower and horses to flaunt its power. Bairi Tusi was unwilling to show weakness and gathered his subordinates and monks to resist with all their strength. In mid-August of this year, the sentries of both sides clashed, followed by a formal declaration of war. Daji Temple sent its cavalry to attack and loot Bairi villages and occupy the houses. Seeing that the situation was unfavorable, Bairi requested assistance from the standing army in Xikang (i.e., Liu Wenhui's subordinates). The standing army had been stationed in a remote area for a long time, living in hardship, and had long coveted the wealth of Daji Temple. Hearing this news, they gladly agreed to provide assistance. However, they were worried that the lamas of Daji Temple were numerous and had sufficient guns, and that they had a long-standing relationship with Tibet. If they lost the battle, they would lose the prestige of the authorities. If they won the battle, they were afraid that the Tibetan side would use the excuse of protecting the temple to intervene. Therefore, they took precautions and first notified the Tibetan army stationed nearby with an official document, explaining the illegal activities of Daji Temple and planning to send troops to suppress them, requesting that they not misunderstand. The Tibetan army replied that the matter was within the jurisdiction of their army and that they would not misunderstand, but requested that they handle it cautiously. Therefore, Ma, the brigade commander of the 24th Army stationed in Da Jianlu, dispatched several companies of troops and brought cannons to join the original garrison in Ganzi to attack Daji Temple. Unexpectedly, the lamas of the temple were well-trained and did not show weakness when they saw the government troops. They counterattacked several times without losing ground. Moreover, the Tibetan army stationed in Dege supplied ammunition, and their momentum became even stronger. The government troops then increased their reinforcements and launched a large-scale encirclement in order to annihilate Daji Temple. Daji Temple had no choice but to retreat and defend the temple fortress, and asked the Dalai Lama for assistance. In order to protect its base for eastward invasion, the Dalai Lama telegraphed the Central Government, requesting that Liu Wenhui stop the troops stationed in Kang from attacking. However, the army had been besieging for several months, but Daji Temple's fortress was strong and there was no result. If they withdrew their troops, they would not only fail to recover their losses, but also lose face. Therefore, even though they had received orders from the Central Government, they still continued to send troops and generals in the hope of winning. However, the inner and outer walls of Daji Temple were about one zhang wide and two zhang high. The temple had enough grain stored to last for three years. With deep trenches and high walls, they were waiting for the enemy in a relaxed manner. It is still doubtful whether the government troops will be able to win. Moreover, the Tibetan army is close at hand, so they are not in a hurry to provide assistance. On the one hand, they want to use the Central Government's order to stop the attack. On the other hand, it is because Daji Temple has the strength to resist. If the government troops continue to reinforce, then the Tibetan side will definitely send troops to help. In that case, the overall situation in Kang and Tibet will turn into a vortex of war, and the national defense in the western border will become increasingly uncontrollable. Moreover, the merchants in the counties of the North Road are not moving forward due to the impact of the war, and business is extremely depressed. The tax revenue in Kangding has also been greatly reduced. Both Han and Tibetan merchants are complaining. It is hoped that the Central Government will issue another strict order to stop military action and seek a proper solution as soon as possible. (November 15th)

Regulations for Investigation Centers Established by the Anti-Opium Association

The Anti-Opium Commission has previously drafted the regulations for the investigation centers in the central government and various provinces and cities in accordance with Article 24 of the Implementing Rules of the Anti-Opium Law and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for approval in order to comply with them. Now, the Executive Yuan has issued an instruction to allow the promulgation. The regulations are recorded as follows: (Article 1) These regulations are formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 24 of the Implementing Rules of the Anti-Opium Law. (Article 2) The Central Investigation Center is directly under the Anti-Opium Commission. The investigation centers in various provinces and cities are directly under the Anti-Opium Commission of the province or city. (Article 3) For civil servants who have been reported or denounced in accordance with the Rules for Investigating Civil Servants, the head of the competent authority shall send a letter to the local Anti-Opium Commission to transfer them for investigation.

(Article 4) The personnel responsible for the investigation are as follows: 1. Director of the Center; 2. Physician; 3. One supervisor from the local Anti-Opium Commission; 4. One supervisor from the competent authority. (Article 5) After the civil servant has been investigated, regardless of whether they have an opium addiction or not, the responsible personnel in the previous article shall sign and affix their seals to the investigation report. (Article 6) All food, clothing, and utensils of the person being investigated during the investigation period shall be inspected by the investigation center. (Article 7) During the investigation period, relatives and friends of the person being investigated are not allowed to visit. If there are special circumstances, the director of the center may handle it at their discretion. (Article 8) The investigation period for the person being investigated shall be limited to five to ten days. (Article 9) After the investigation of the person being investigated is completed, the investigation center shall send the investigation report together with the person being investigated to the Anti-Opium Commission for verification. (Article 10) The investigation center shall have one director and two to three physicians (the director shall be concurrently appointed by personnel from the Anti-Opium Commission at all levels; the physician shall be selected and appointed by the Anti-Opium Commission upon request of the director). (Article 11) In order to draft documents and handle other affairs, the director may employ a number of employees at their discretion. (Article 12) If any staff member or supervisor of the investigation center is found to be engaging in favoritism or deception, they shall be severely punished according to the law, regardless of whether they are still in office or have left office. (Article 13) The detailed rules for the operation of the investigation center shall be formulated by the center and submitted to the Anti-Opium Commission for approval. (Article 14) These regulations shall come into effect on the date of promulgation.

Local Communications

Songjiang

The First District Office Handles Land Clearance: The First District Office was ordered to handle land clearance. The district chief concurrently serves as the director of land clearance and has been issued forms and other documents and is eager to start implementation. At the 16th district affairs meeting on the 20th, it was decided to investigate the population. The district office will distribute various population investigation forms to the heads of villages and towns and start the investigation immediately, with a deadline of one month for completion. All compilation and investigation fees, in addition to the one cent per household stipulated by the county government, will be supplemented with an additional two cents per household for writing and ordering house numbers. The house numbers in the entire district will be compiled separately by the village and town heads as units, numbered from east to west. The house numbers will be made of lead sheet and will be provided and distributed by the district office. During the investigation, the district will instruct the village and town police and notify the sub-stations to send police to assist.

Recent News on the Construction of the Seawall Project: The Jinshanwei seawall along the coast of Punan in this county has been collapsing repeatedly and is very dangerous. In March of this year, the provincial government decided to start construction using new methods and building with cement. Commissioner Sun Kaiyi was appointed to supervise the project. The project cost is estimated at 75,000 yuan and is contracted by the Shanghai Xinyutai Construction Factory. It is reported that it will be completed by March next year.

Kunshan

Student Unrest at Qiandun Central Elementary School: Since Sun Yongchun took over as principal of Qiandun Central Elementary School this semester, he has been enthusiastic in his work. However, some of the teachers he hired, such as Zheng, Lu, and Tang, are of low academic attainment and young and impetuous. If students ask questions or stammer in their answers, they will be severely punished. Therefore, whenever Zheng teaches, the students are unwilling to listen. The most bizarre punishment is that boarding students who violate school rules will have their lunch or dinner stopped. Therefore, students often cry with empty stomachs, which has aroused the indignation of various families, who have jointly requested the Education Bureau to replace the bad teachers. However, Zheng and others not only did not repent, but intensified their actions, taking their anger out on the students, and beating and scolding them without asking for the reason in order to vent their anger. The parents, unable to bear their children being humiliated for no reason, had no choice but to order their children to temporarily suspend their studies.

After learning about this, the Education Bureau immediately sent county inspector Xu Shaolie and Education Committee member Zhou Qichao to Qiandun to investigate the truth. The parents and students confessed everything and requested the education authorities to immediately replace Zheng and others. Xu and Zhou saw that the facts were clear and promised to report the real situation to the director of the bureau, hoping that the education authorities would have a good solution.

Suzhou

Zhao Yihe Rice Shop Closes Due to Debt: Zhao Yihe Rice Shop on Xumen Zao City Street has been open for more than 60 years and suddenly declared bankruptcy yesterday (20th). The manager, Zhao Fuchu (Mianyun), who is also the owner, has fled. The total amount of debt owed to the assistant manager, Wu Heling, is about 130,000 yuan, including 10,000 yuan owed to Shenyuzhuang and 30,000 to 40,000 yuan owed to Xiefengsheng, Dayi, and Dayikang. The remaining 80,000 to 90,000 yuan is owed to small depositors. It is reported that the reason for the bankruptcy is that business has been sluggish for many years and there were losses of more than 10,000 yuan in wheat this year. Zhao himself lost 20,000 yuan in Shanghai by speculating in gold. Moreover, the store was originally managed by his father, Zhao Shucheng. After Shucheng passed away eight years ago, Fuchu was addicted to writing and contributing to newspapers in Shanghai and was not good at managing the business. Over the years, there have been losses to partners and customers, and the accumulated losses have been too great, resulting in financial difficulties. Zhao Qian Dadaou Hang (managed by Shi Weichun and assisted by Pan Jianting), an affiliated store of the store in Darihui Bridge, was also asked by depositors to withdraw their goods as collateral yesterday. In addition, there is a branch of Zhao Yihe in Pingwang, but the business is not large enough to be worth mentioning.

Pirates Rob Farmers: A few nights ago, many sea bandits arrived at He Village in Changshu County and robbed the homes of villagers such as Zhou. After looting, the bandits fled into the Yangtze River. Afterwards, the captain of the first detachment of the 13th water police team rushed to pursue them and reported to the third water police district yesterday (20th) requesting arrest.

The High Court Executes a Murderer: Xiao Lao, a native of Taixing, and his wife Zhao had known their neighbor Zhou Jixiang for a long time. At that time, Xiao Lao was experiencing financial difficulties and was repeatedly assisted by Zhou Jixiang. Until March of the 13th year of the Republic of China, Xiao planned to take Zhao and his son Que'er to Huzhou. When Zhou heard about this, he also wanted to go to Jiangnan to make a living with his younger brother Zhou Zhishan and apprentice Song Genqing. They hired Zhu Genyi's boat together on March 3rd of the same year. When they reached the middle of the river, Zhou Jixiang recalled that Zhao had been having an affair with him for many years and had spent a lot of money, so he demanded 60 yuan from Xiao, which led to a dispute. Zhou Jixiang immediately cut Xiao's hand with a knife and pushed him into the river. The boatman Zhu Genyi rescued him and brought him back on board before he died. When the boat docked, Zhou claimed that he would accompany Xiao Lao to Changzhou for treatment and ordered his apprentice Song Genqing to carry him to the beach. Zhou then used a knife to stab Xiao to death. The Changzhou police arrested Zhou and brought him to the county for trial. He was sentenced to death. Zhou refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the High Court, which also sentenced him to death. Zhou still refused to accept the judgment and appealed to the Supreme Court, which also rejected his appeal. A few days ago, the Supreme Court Prosecutor's Office ordered the High Court Prosecutor's Office to execute Zhou Jixiang. After receiving the order, the High Prosecutor's Office ordered Prosecutor Zhu Wenzhuo to go to the Sijian Street Third Prison execution ground at 7:00 a.m. yesterday (20th) and order the bailiff to bring Zhou Jixiang to confirm his identity and execute him by hanging according to the law.

Wuxi

Kidnapping Case: Bandits Intimidate Victim: At the intersection of Jingyun and Taibo markets in this county, a place called Xiaoqiaotou, a large number of lake bandits armed with weapons robbed and kidnapped seven men during the Mid-Autumn Festival of the lunar calendar this year. Two of them were later released. Afterwards, police detectives from this county cracked the case in Shanghai and arrested 19 bandits. Two hostages were also rescued by the Shanghai police. The other three hostages were hidden by the bandits in another boat and escaped without a trace. Recently, the bandits sent another letter to the victim Ling Dixiang, stating that the sender has received the four letters from the main force. They were waiting for the designated representatives to come to negotiate an agreement. If they desired a settlement, they should send the agreed amount to a specific location and not self-sabotage. Ling ignored the letter after receiving it. It was said that several days ago Ling Yuanxiang said that the bandits sent a letter saying that the bandits guarding the hostages were suffering, and that the boats the bandits were on were now located at Jiangyin.

Police and Bandits Engage in Fierce Battle in Taihu Lake: Recently, bandits have been discovered in Taihu Lake, in the Dongting West Mountain area, robbing civilian boats and kidnapping people for ransom. Wang Shengwu, the captain of the 8th water police team stationed in Dongshan, learned of this and led a team to suppress them. They encountered the bandits at Mingwan, and saw four bandit boats with eighty or ninety bandits armed with guns. Captain Wang immediately joined forces with the 3rd district water police of Jiangsu and the local militia to engage the bandits in a fierce battle for four hours. The bandit forces are running low. Some of them are in Xiaogang. The police are now searching and dividing them up. Yesterday, Captain Wang telegraphed the situation of the bandit suppression to Mao Mujun, the district director of the 2nd water police district stationed . After receiving the telegram, Mao immediately ordered the Zhaowu warship to sail to Taihu Lake to assist in the encirclement and suppression, striving to annihilate all of the bandits.

Changshu

A Traditional Chinese Doctor, Zhang Chengqi, Escapes from a Bandit Den and Returns to His Hometown: Zhang Chengqi, a traditional Chinese doctor practicing in Xiyangzhen in the mountain area, was kidnapped together with Zhang Baoqi and three others by the bandit Zou Quixuan last month. The bandits, via Da'an Port, sent a letter to Zhang's family demanding a ransom of four thousand yuan. When the family went to pay the ransom, the bandits demanded seven thousand yuan to release Zhang and the others at the same time. Zhang's family, lacking such a large sum and having no connection with Zhang Baoqi and the others, couldn't fulfill the demand. The bandits insisted on the joint ransom of seven thousand yuan because they were unwilling to release Zhang. Zhang, who had been practicing traditional Chinese medicine for decades and was well-known in the Xiyang and Fushan area, was asked by the bandits to be their resident doctor after being kidnapped. The bandits treated Zhang extremely well, providing him with separate room and assigning several bandits to serve him in shifts, while still keeping him under surveillance, albeit loosely. Zhang, seeking to escape his captivity, feigned compliance with the bandits. Recently, the counties of Tongzhou and Haizhou launched a large-scale campaign to suppress the bandits, resulting in fierce fighting for two days and nights. The bandits, unable to withstand the assault, retreated to Songji Port. The bandit leader was arrested, and the bandit gang fell into disarray. Zhang seized the opportunity to escape, fleeing for dozens of miles without rest. He arrived in Nantong territory on the 18th and then took a boat back home. It is reported that Zhang will rest for a few days before resuming his practice to make a living. Zhang Baoqi and the others are still in danger.

Yao Weicai Commits Suicide by Drinking Tranquilizing Medicine: Yao Weicai, a shareholder of Yifengchang Sugar Store outside Xiaodongmen in this county, was thirty-three years old. He lost his father at a young age and was raised by his aunt. He later studied in Kunshan and returned to join Xiao Fuchang, Lu Fengshan, and others to open a sugar store. Initially, Yao was solely responsible for management, but due to losses, Lu was made manager instead. Yao was only in charge of economic income and expenses, and his father-in-law was asked to introduce and guarantee loans from the money shop. Unexpectedly, Xiao and Lu colluded to embezzle accounts and funds. As the end of the year approached, Yao, seeing no hope for the store's development, planned to commit suicide. On the evening of the 18th, he still had dinner at home before going to the store to sleep. The next morning, when Yao did not wake up, they went to call him, only to find him barely breathing and unresponsive. Realizing something was wrong, they informed his wife, Cao, who rushed over and found two bottles of tranquilizing medicine. It was then they knew he had taken poison. They quickly called a Western doctor to save him, but it was in vain. He died at around nine o'clock. His wife, Cao, knowing the inside story of the store and suspecting that her husband's suicide was related to Xiao and Lu, went to the Public Security Bureau to report the matter. Xiao and Lu were arrested and taken to the county judicial office. At two o'clock in the afternoon, the trial officer, Shen Hengsheng, opened the court for interrogation. According to Cao's statement, Yao Weicai left a handwritten grievance document consisting of thirteen pages before his death. Interrogating Lu and Xiao revealed that they were likely involved. They were ordered to be released on bail. Cao was allowed to arrange the burial of the body first.

Jiyuan became enraged and threw an orange at his wife's head. Instantly, brain matter gushed out, and she fell to the ground and died. Kong, realizing his recklessness, immediately went to the kitchen and tried to cut his throat with a kitchen knife, but he was stopped by neighbors. He has now become insane.

The meeting decided that the settlement date for the city would follow the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's decision to set February 15, 20, as the final date for receiving and returning debts for this session. It was also decided that businesses would be closed for two days on the first and second days of the New Year in the 20th year. The meeting then adjourned.

The Bandit Suppression Headquarters is About to Be Abolished: The City's Four Prefecture Bandit Suppression Headquarters has been in operation for more than three years, with the commander concurrently serving as the director of the Zhejiang Water Police Bureau, Wang Wenhan. It is now reported that Commander-in-Chief Chiang telegraphed that the task of bandit suppression in the three provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang should be the responsibility of the Pacification Supervisor and the Security Offices of each province, as the rebels have been cleared. Therefore, the City's Four Prefecture Bandit Suppression Headquarters will be abolished.

Doctor Ma Dasan Barely Escapes Yuyao: It was reported that Doctor Ma Dasan of Yubei, Yuyao, was kidnapped by bandits last month. It is now learned that the Northeast District Security Group of the county snatched back the hostage Ma Dasan from the bandits at Dahu Gate, Sitangnan the other day, and captured four bandits and twelve pistols, which have been sent to the county government for review.

Public Security Bureau Investigator Flees Ningbo After Bending the Law: After a tip-off from citizens Wang Agan and Zhong Tongzhang, Yin Kui, an investigator from the Ningbo Public Security Bureau, went to the Xiehe Southern Goods Store opened by a Fujianese on Houtang Street in Jiangdong to search for opium. As a result, they found three packages of opium and smoking paraphernalia, as well as three pistols under the bed. Seeing that things were not going well, the store owner bribed the investigator with two hundred yuan. The investigator returned one of the pistols and privately pocketed the other two, fearing that Wang and Zhong, who had gone with him, would leak the matter. At the time, he gave Wang and Zhong twenty yuan each. Unexpectedly, someone later reported the matter to the detective team. The team, upon receiving the report, dispatched detectives to arrest Wang and Zhong first and summoned Wang Zhengjing, a witness from Xiehe Company, to the case. They were transferred to the Public Security Bureau for strict handling, while Investigator Yin Kui fled upon hearing the news and is currently being hunted down.

A Fire in Taizhu District, Zhenhai: At about 5 o'clock yesterday morning, a fire broke out at Chen Zhengquan's house in Chenzhong Fu Gehe, Taizhu District, Zhenhai, because he was careless about fire prevention. It spread to the neighboring houses of Chen Caixiang, Chen Guisheng, and Chen Aisheng, destroying seven houses with buildings, two alleys, one row of flat houses, and four or five small houses, as well as more than 7,000 catties of grain, with a total loss of more than 5,000 yuan. When the fire broke out, Chen Zhengquan tried to put out the fire with all his might, but he was burned all over his body and was seriously injured. He has been sent to the hospital for treatment.

Hangzhou

The Economic Committee Decides to Abolish: Former Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Renjie, due to the province's financial situation reaching a dead end, specially organized the Zhejiang Provincial Government Economic Committee, inviting economic experts from the province as members to pool their wisdom and benefit from it to restore Zhejiang's finance and enable various undertakings to directly and indirectly receive good influences. After its establishment, regulations were formulated and meetings were held, which have already shown some progress. Recently, after the reorganization of the provincial government, the new chairman, Zhang Nanxian, in order to implement austerity policies, submitted a proposal to the meeting to abolish this committee. In addition, construction agencies are also planning to be merged to save expenses.

The Provincial Government Appoints Heads of Water and Land Police Bureaus: Zhao Zihe, the head of the Zhejiang Inland River Water Police Bureau, submitted a request to the provincial government to resign from his position. After deliberation by the provincial government meeting, it was decided that the vacancy would be filled by Liu Zuhan, the current commander of the Jiangbei Bandit Suppression Guerrilla Force. Zhu Yi, the head of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, was ordered to go to Japan to investigate police administration, and the vacancy has been filled by He Yun to take charge, making use of his expertise.

Transitional Measures for the End of the Year in Zhejiang Province: Provincial Government Chairman Zhang Nanxian, acting concurrently as Finance Director Wang Zhengying, stated that the end of the year is approaching and that expenses of 2.47 million yuan are required for the New Year. After many days of deliberation, it has been learned that a solution was decided yesterday. It is proposed that construction funds (stored and awaiting allocation of special funds and bonds) be temporarily borrowed from the Construction Department by the Finance Department. Once the New Year is over, the counties will have collected taxes and will make up the funds. However, because it concerns the progress of construction projects, it must be implemented after seeking the consent of former Chairman Zhang.

Correspondence

Correspondence from the Ministry of Railways

Dear Editor,

Having read your newspaper's report on the 18th of this month, in the Xuzhou dispatch, it was said that "(Jinpu Bureau Director Sun Hegao, accompanied by Railway Department Vice Minister Lian Shenghai, passed through Xuzhou on the 19th morning en route to Tianjin)." Upon investigation, this does not correspond with the facts. Our department's Vice Minister Lian did not leave the department that day. The report in your newspaper that he passed through Xuzhou en route to Tianjin is an erroneous report.

Accordingly, we request that you promptly make a correction.

Secretariat of the Ministry of Railways, December 19th.

Special Educational News

Life at Wellesley College

(1)

(Sent from the United States by Ms. Lu Erzhao of Songjiang)

(1) Overview of the School

It seems advisable for women seeking education in the United States to go to this school first.

Wellesley College is located in Meigen Province, USA. The school covers an area of more than 600 acres. The newly built buildings are grand in scale and complete in equipment. The library, laboratories, gymnasium, and auditorium are particularly emphasized as the source of the four aspects of education: moral, intellectual, physical, and aesthetic. The curriculum is divided into departments such as education, literature, home economics, sociology, theology, mathematics, physics, chemistry, physical education, law, and political science, with more students in the education, literature, home economics, sociology, and theology departments. Each classroom has a clock and the school regulations stipulate that if a student is one minute late, the professor must record it and report it to the office. Teachers can be up to a quarter of an hour late, but teachers and students are never late.

It goes without saying that the teaching in each department is rigorous, and special attention is paid to mutual assistance, service, and physical fitness training.

(A) Training in Mutual Assistance and Service: At the three prayer meetings each week, there must be a lecture on the ancient events and principles of mutual assistance and service, nothing more than embracing the spirit of Christ (I serve others, not others serve me). Teachers use this to teach students, and students use this to learn. If you immerse yourself in it for a long time, you will be able to change your temperament. Although there are many enthusiastic public welfare and mutual assistance service facts in our country recently, there are also those who regard local public interests as the moonlight in front of the window and the frost on the roof tiles, and push them away without caring. There are many selfish and self-interested people in the Western countries, but they are often regarded by society as Jews (a synonym for slaves of the country). The causes of the environment are different, and the results of the nation are also different. Those who are engaged in educational positions should carefully study it.

(B) Compulsory Physical Training: Ball games and freehand exercises are of course practiced conscientiously, and practical tests in the swimming pool are regarded as major subjects. The president's advocacy, the teacher's training, the encouragement of points, and the students' hard work, coupled with the exquisite equipment in the pool that attracts people, make the swimming pleasure arise unconsciously. This is true for American women. Japanese people are mostly known for their swimming skills. Students from my alma mater, both Chinese and Western, often become healthier after a year of studying here. Therefore, a female physical education professor said with a smile to Yu that after graduating and returning to China in a few years, she did not recognize her mother because she was so strong. The teacher is probably proud of the physical education progress of each student.

This school is one of the pure women's universities in the United States. It was founded earlier, and there are more graduates. Ms. Wang Xi of Wusong, is known for her intelligence. Her aunt and niece both graduated from this school. The wife of Dr. Meng of Huzhou also graduated from this school. Next year (1931), her daughter will also make an appointment to study at this school. There are more than a dozen alumni from the Shanghai Zhongxi School who have come here, most of whom have graduated and returned to China to serve. This school has a reputation for treating Chinese people favorably. It seems advisable for women seeking education in the United States to go to this school first.

(2) Teacher Attitude

Most of the teachers are women, many of whom are old, respected, white-haired, wrinkled, experienced, and have excellent teaching methods. When they take the stage to lecture, they are energetic, their words are calm, and in important places, they often go over them again and again, ordering each student to find the key points themselves and strive to solve them automatically. Only when each student can know where the knot is and thoroughly understand it will they stop patiently teaching. Their spirit of never tiring of teaching is truly enough to make each student sincerely admire them. During the exam, they choose to ask questions about the essentials, and if each student can analyze and answer in detail, they will give full marks. Some people say that the reason why each teacher is so sincere in their guidance and never slackens is because they hold the doctrine of love for people, the doctrine of service, that is, the doctrine of sacrifice. They often said to each student that if you have talent, knowledge, and experience but no love for people, service, and sacrifice, then your innate talent, all your knowledge, and experience are equal to castles in the air, useless and may even harm society. These few words are also regarded as mottos by Erzhao. Erzhao carefully considers why each teacher at this school is so earnest: one is because they hold religious doctrines, two is that female teachers have special care for female students, and three is that each teacher regards education as a lifelong career, liking it and enjoying it. If they initially regard the school as a post office or a rain shelter, they will not take the school as a means of earning a living and do things perfunctorily for the students.

Important News

Ministry of Education Promulgates Elementary School Student

Group Organization Guidelines

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued a circular to the provincial education departments and municipal education bureaus promulgating four key points for the organization of elementary school student groups, ordering them to instruct the schools to comply with the order. The order stated that the principles for the organization of student groups had already been promulgated by the Central Training Department in Document No. 12083. However, according to Article 6 of these principles, the organization of elementary school student groups does not apply to these regulations. Therefore, there should be separate regulations regarding the organization of elementary school student groups. The Ministry has repeatedly received requests from party departments at all levels to provide regulations, and it has also approved the Central Secretariat's transfer of the reports of your Ministry to the provincial education departments requesting instructions. Now, the Ministry has formulated four key points for the organization of elementary school student groups. We are enclosing a copy of these key points and ask your Ministry to review them and implement them accordingly, and to reply to us. The Central Training Department's letter of approval for the transmission of the key points for the organization of elementary school student groups to the knowledge of the instructions is enclosed, along with an order to comply accordingly, and for the benefit of etc., a copy of the aforementioned key points is copied and issued to the knowledge of the instructions, and to inform the affiliated elementary schools to comply with this order.

Key Points for the Organization of Elementary School Student Groups

1. Scope: Limited to organizations within the school.

2. Purpose: To use the spirit of the Three Principles of the People to enable students to practice independent living, promote a spirit of mutual assistance, and increase service capabilities and interest to promote the development of their moral, intellectual, physical, and group education.

3. Name and Method: Must be adapted to the local student environment and not be bound by the uniformity of names and methods.

4. Supervision: Subject to the guidance and supervision of the school.

Chinese Meteorological Society Holds Annual Meeting

Held in Beijing Today

The Chinese Meteorological Society was founded in the thirteenth year of the Republic of China. With the recent advancements in aviation, the society's work has become increasingly developed. In addition to the major meteorological institutions across the country, the Aviation Administration of the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of Transportation, and the Shanghai-Chengdu Aviation Administration have all joined as group members of the society. The number of members at home and abroad has reached 150. The convocation of this year's National Meteorological Conference was also a decision made at the society's annual meeting last year. It has now been learned that the society is scheduled to hold its sixth annual meeting on December 21st at the China Science Society on Chengxian Street in Nanjing. The papers that have been received and are proposed to be read at the meeting include: (1) Zhu Wenrong's observations of upper-level airflow in Nanjing, (2) Zheng Zizheng's study of monsoons in China, (3) Lu Hongtu's study of the colloidality of air, (4) Zhu Binghai's research on frost. There are also more than ten proposals to be decided at the meeting. The itinerary is as follows: 9:00 AM: Opening ceremony; 2: Speech by the chairman; 3: Report on the society's affairs by the secretary-general; 4: Speeches; 5: Reading of papers; 6: Photography. 12:00 PM: Banquet of the Chinese Meteorological Society. 2:00 PM: 1. The chairman announces the results of the election of the president, vice president, and the location of the Council and the Secretariat; 2. Election of directors and secretary-general; 3. Discussion of proposals. 6:00 PM: Banquet of the Meteorological Research Institute of the National Central Research Institute.

Yang Yongnian Obtains Doctorate in Medicine in Japan

United News Agency, Tokyo, 20th: Yang Yongnian, a 30-year-old Chinese student, submitted a thesis to Keio Medical University and was approved and awarded a doctorate in medicine today. The main papers he submitted were (Research on the Antibacterial Effect of Oxidized Light) (The Effect of [Omitted] Soda on the Sterilization and Bacterial Growth of Oxidized Light). Mr. Yang was originally an assistant at the South Manchuria Railway Medical College and later became a South Manchuria Railway student. He is a graduate student in the Department of Medicine at Keio University and has completed the curriculum of the Department of Bacteriology. He is currently a specially selected research fellow of the Cultural Affairs Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs.

Local News

Jiaotong University Held Groundbreaking Ceremony for Engineering Building Yesterday

Since Sun Zhesheng and Li Rousheng took over the leadership of National Jiaotong University, they have spared no effort to expand the content. Recently, the school's construction funds approved by the Ministry have reached more than 550,000 yuan, the most important of which is the construction of the Engineering Building. After the funds were warned, the school immediately solicited bids, and the result was contracted by Fuchi. At 12:30 noon yesterday, the school specially held a groundbreaking ceremony for the Engineering Building. Minister Sun was unable to come to the school temporarily due to something, and President Li Zhaohuan wielded the hoe to perform the ceremony and reported on everything. Finally, Professor Hu Dunfu gave a speech. The main points of the speeches of Li and Hu are as follows:

President Li reported in brief that the construction, equipment, and machinery costs of the Engineering Building to be built by the school this time are about 600,000 yuan. In recent years, the Ministry's funds have been stretched. The early commencement of the school's Engineering Building is both in accordance with the Ministry of Education's intention to expand the content and due to Minister Sun's efforts to raise funds. It is expected that the building can be completed in August next year and all the renovations can be completed between September and October. It is planned to hold the opening ceremony of the building at the same time as the school's 35th anniversary. The interior of the Engineering Building is divided into three floors. The lower floor is planned to be an electrical engineering laboratory, a materials laboratory, a mechanical laboratory, and a metalworking factory. The second floor will be used for two large classrooms, a drawing classroom, the offices of the various deans, a teacher's lounge, and an instrument room. The third floor will not be built for the time being and is planned to be added later when funds are sufficient. A circular open space is left in the building to prepare for the future addition of engineering or science and railway museums. Such a grand engineering building is rare in China. After the completion of this building next year, the school's reputation can be increased, and it will also meet the Ministry of Education's intention to enrich the content. The completion of this building will also make a great contribution to China's engineering science in the future. With this good material environment, the students of this school must also strive for knowledge in the spiritual aspect, etc.

Dr. Hu Dunfu's speech. Hu briefly stated that the commencement of the school's engineering project this time can be the foundation for all new construction in the school. He hoped that the students would study hard and not let down the party-state's cultivation of talents and the earnest expectations of the authorities, etc.

Declaration by Guanghua Students Regarding the Current Situation

(National News Agency) Guanghua University students of this city, including Li Jing and 251 others, declared: "We came to Shanghai to study at Guanghua University, considering it one of the leading universities by the sea. It emerged from the cultural encroachment of imperialism (John), shedding its Fumin facade and possessing a glorious revolutionary history. Unexpectedly, in recent years, those in charge have been unsuitable. Allowing the Nationalist faction to thrive, they regard figures like Lin Cheng, who collaborates with powerful figures, as their stronghold. Since Liao Shicheng, a running dog of Sun Chuanfang, the warlord of Dongda University, and a supporter of the Five-Colored Flag Datong League, became the president, he has gathered his cronies and occupied key positions, such as Luo Longji, Zhu Qinglai, and Shen Youqian. They usually advocate theories of freedom and constitutionalism to oppose the government and criticize the authorities, thereby misleading students. Each adheres to his own interpretation of freedom, but when it comes to university affairs, they suppress and prohibit without reason. The promotion of party ideology education is evident in the resolutions of the Third National Congress and the orders of party and government organs, even down to the elementary schools. However, Guanghua, a university with a glorious revolutionary history, not only lacks courses on party ideology but also never holds memorial weeks. The unity of knowledge and action, an old saying of Wang Yangming, runs contrary to 'knowledge is easy but action is difficult,' which has long been refuted by the Premier. Anyone with a little understanding of party ideology can tell this. Yet, Liao Shicheng not only deviates from his teacher's teachings but also brazenly imparts training and education to students, just as Tao Zhihxing, a prominent Nationalist faction member, did at Xiaozhuang School. How can we not feel that we are not alone and that we will be compared favorably in the future? Since Liao has followed in Tao's footsteps, Guanghua will inevitably end up like Xiaozhuang. The thought fills us with dread. Previously, local party and government organs investigated and confirmed the situation, reported it to the Ministry of Education, which issued a reprimand and ordered rectification. However, Liao simply laughed it off, as if he saw nothing. His betrayal of the spirit of party ideology education is enough to exemplify the rest. Even from the standpoint of the Nationalist faction itself, this is understandable. But look at today's church schools, which even add courses on party ideology and observe memorial weeks. It is unbelievable that Guanghua, which emerged from opposing the church, is so absurd. What difference is there between Guanghua and John? Guanghua should be ashamed, while John is laughing at it. We, as students, witness this and feel heartbroken. For the sake of loving our school, we cannot remain silent. But speaking out is often suppressed with the excuse that students cannot interfere in university affairs. Remaining silent would be a betrayal of our conscience. Enduring this reactionary education of the Nationalist faction day after day without being able to clear ourselves is truly heartbreaking, and we cannot help but sigh deeply for the future of party ideology education. This time, the Nanfeng Society and the Lanling Society had a dispute over a soccer game. Liao, because he despised the shamelessness of the Nationalist faction and refused to be exploited by them, harbors resentment towards the Nanfeng Society and secretly instructs his running dogs to deliberately sow discord, causing the conflict between the two sides to escalate, thereby creating an opportunity to eliminate dissidents. His means are more ruthless than Zheng Zhuang Gong. As expected, within a few days, expulsion orders were issued, and ten innocent classmates were sacrificed. Yang Shuchun is not even a member of the Nanfeng Society, but simply because he is a standing committee member of a district branch, he was also sacrificed as a collateral victim. Such perverse actions cause people to feel bewildered and uneasy. Liao's party of rebellious students then seized the opportunity to run amok, arbitrarily disregarding everything. Slogans and shouts such as '(Down with the Kuomintang),' '(Down with Chiang Kai-shek),' and '(Long live Nationalism)' filled the air, and Communist leaflets were also flying around. Seeing this behavior, we felt that we could no longer tolerate it. However, we still did not want to deviate from the normal course. On the one hand, we expressed our opinions to President Zhang, demanding the expulsion of Nationalist faction teachers and staff such as Liao Shicheng and Luo Longji. On the other hand, we united with our classmates and waited quietly for a solution. We disdained the most inferior actions such as strikes, coercion, external declarations, and exaggeration in the hope of escalating the situation. Therefore, although there was a proposal for a strike declaration among the students at that time, the fact that we unanimously opposed and rejected it is enough to prove our attitude. However, Liao knew that the situation had become unmanageable and that the facts were undeniable. Therefore, he tried his best to instigate his private party teachers to distort the facts and issue declarations in order to shift the blame to the students and avoid social condemnation. Little did he know that he was trying to cover up his heinous crimes. A dispute over soccer is a matter between students. There is no need to expel a large number of students. And expelling students is a matter for the school. There is no need to issue external declarations. Yet, he uses dangerous words and exaggerates the situation. Whether this kind of provocative action violates the orders of the Executive Yuan, the world will have its own judgment. The responsibility for the escalation of the situation lies with him. We were originally waiting quietly for a solution. However, since the reactionary faction teachers have already distorted the facts, we cannot allow them to slander us. Therefore, we are making the truth public to set the record straight. In short, we started with loving our school and will end with loving our school. We started with expelling Liao and will end with expelling Liao. If we do not achieve the goal of thoroughly expelling all Nationalist factions in the school, we would rather be shattered jade than preserved tile. We hope that people from all walks of life will rise up and help us." Guanghua University students Li Jing and 251 others.

Preparations for Jinan Football Team's Expedition to the Philippines

Departing on January 6 to Participate in Charity Matches

Farewell Ceremony for the Zhenru Basketball Team Tomorrow, Who Will Also Be Traveling

Since the National Jinan University Football Team received a formal invitation from the Philippine Sports Association, representing the government of that country, to participate in charity and carnival matches, Director of Physical Education Chen Zhang'e and Coach Wu Yanzhang have been actively preparing for departure.

Participating in Charity Matches

The team will leave Shanghai on January 6 and arrive in Manila on the 12th. The match schedule has not yet been finalized, but the charity matches will generally be held from January 15 to 18. In the week or so before and after these four days, Jinan's interest in soccer matches has been very high lately. Jinan's trip carries the name of national representative, and the warm welcome it will receive from overseas Chinese can be imagined. The strong opponents in the charity matches will include the university teams of Santo Tomas University, Sarasa University, and Anthony University. In addition, there will be the Narmada team organized by the British, the Cacheño team from Spain, and the Philippine team.

Will Compete in Hong Kong Upon Return

Whether to continue participating in the Carnival after the closing of the charity matches will be determined based on the circumstances at that time. If the entire team returns to the country, it is planned to leave the Philippines on the Canadian Empress on January 28. When passing through Hong Kong, they will land and compete with China or Nanhua before going to Guangzhou, where Huang Dengqiu and Dr. Situ You will be in charge of the arrangements. By the time they arrive in Shanghai, the elite players of the team may be able to contribute to the Chinese team for the World Soccer Cup.

Farewell Reception Tomorrow

The Philippine Overseas Chinese Student Association of the school has scheduled a dance party at the Dahua Hotel Ballroom on Gordon Road from 4 PM to 8:30 PM tomorrow. The program will be quite spectacular. In addition, a special edition of the expedition to the Philippines will be published, with rich content planned by Mr. Cai Guoping and others.

French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association Held Citizens Representative Assembly Yesterday

Welcoming the New Chinese Directors and Committee Members to Office

Successively Expressing Municipal Opinions

The French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association held a citizens' representative assembly at the Shandong Guild Hall on Ximen Road at 3 PM yesterday to welcome the French Municipal Council's Chinese directors and committee members to office. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded below:

Attendees: Cheng Zhusong, Gong Jingyan, Shang Mujiang, Chen Dezhang, Jin Liren, Wei Tingrong, Xu Xiuting, Wu Shijun, Xu Qingrong, Li Weiliang, Zai Chunfeng, Sun Ruiting, Lu Tingjian, Bei Zairong, Rong Shenghuan (represented by Zhang Zhengang), Tong Lizhang, Dong Kechang, Zhang Qi, Lu Bohong, Zhu Yan, Pan Zhaocun, Yu Zicheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Jin Tingsun, Li Yingsheng, Zhang Yishu, Zhou Qinpu, Lu Rongzhang, Tao Leqin, Wu Liangsheng, Chen Pinlu, Lin Zhengtang (represented by Yu Jingqing), and 33 others (in order of appearance).

Welcoming Procedures: (1) Ringing the bell to open the meeting; (2) All attendees take their seats; (3) Public election of the chairman; (4) Paying the highest respects to the Party and National Flags and the portrait of the Premier; (5) Reading aloud the Premier's will; (6) All representatives welcome the directors and committee members by bowing to each other; (7) The chairman delivers a welcoming speech on behalf of the citizens; (8) The Chinese directors and committee members express their opinions; (9) Commemorative photograph; (10) Tea and refreshments, adjournment.

Meeting Proceedings: The meeting began at 4 PM. After the formalities, master of ceremonies Tong Lizhang publicly nominated Zhang Xiaolin, Cheng Zhusong, and Shang Mujiang as the presiding committee. Chairman Cheng delivered a welcoming speech and then invited the Chinese directors and committee members to express their opinions. Chinese directors Lu Bohong, Zhu Yan, Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Wei Tingrong, and Chinese committee members Shang Mujiang, Zhang Yishu, Cheng Zhusong, Jin Liren, Gong Jingyan, Chen Dezhang, Li Yingsheng, and Zai Chunfeng spoke one after another, mostly offering words of encouragement. Lu Bohong detailed the changes that the Municipal Council should undergo to follow the trend, and Zhu Yan reported on the Municipal Council's promotion of Chinese education, saying that if Chinese citizens have any opinions, please submit them to the Municipal Council. Zhang Xiaolin explained the reasons why the Municipal Council should use Chinese to facilitate the Chinese people, and Shang Mujiang spoke about the opinions of Chinese directors and committee members working together. Committee member Jin Liren then stood up to express his gratitude. The ceremony concluded at around 6 PM with a commemorative photograph and adjournment.

Citizen's Expression: The entire citizenry of the French Concession believes that the French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association's election of five Chinese directors and nine committee members to the Municipal Council to implement participation in municipal power is in line with the principle of equality between China and France and fulfills the expectations of the Chinese citizens. Therefore, various businesses have expressed enthusiastic welcome, and flags are hung on all roads to celebrate, expressing the sincerity of the citizens. Even the alert slogans are enough to show a glimpse of the citizens' wishes.

Brief Biographies of the Directors and Committee Members: Zhang Xiaolin, 54 years old, from Hangxian, Zhejiang Province, is a counselor of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, an advisor to the Deputy Commander-in-Chief, chairman of the Shanghai French Concession General Association, chairman of the Taxpaying Chinese Association, and a director of the French Municipal Council. Du Yuesheng, 43 years old, from Shanghai, Jiangsu Province, is a counselor of the General Headquarters of the Army, Navy, and Air Force, an advisor to the Deputy Commander-in-Chief, chairman of the Shanghai French Concession Business General Association, a committee member of the Taxpaying Chinese Association, a supervisor of the Taxpaying Chinese Association, chairman of the China Exchange Bank, and a director of the French Municipal Council. Zhu Yan, 45 years old, from Shanghai, Jiangsu Province, holds a doctorate in science from the Belgian University of Liège, served as a section chief and secretary of the Ministry of Education, and was the supervisor of Chinese students in Europe and the principal of the Sino-French National Vocational School. He is currently the director of the Shanghai Municipal Land Bureau and a director of the French Concession Municipal Council. Lu Bohong, 56 years old, from Shanghai, Jiangsu Province, was an attaché during the Qing Dynasty and has handled Sino-French cooperative public welfare and charitable undertakings. He has received honorary medals from the French government and is currently the general manager of the Shanghai Chinese Electric Company, a managing director of the Shanghai Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, a standing director of the Shanghai Inland Water Company, the general manager of the Shanghai Datong Renji Shipping Company, a director of the Beiping Central Hospital, the chief director of the Shanghai Xinpu Yutang, the president of the Shanghai Sacred Heart Hospital, the president of the Shanghai Catholic Action Association, and a director of the Shanghai French Concession Municipal Council. Shang Mujiang, 45 years old, from Hangxian, Zhejiang Province, graduated from Zhejiang Japanese Language School, served as the former director of the Zhejiang National Assembly Hall, the principal of Zhejiang Commercial Vocational School, and a secretary of both the Senate and the House of Representatives. He is the chief of preparation for the Taxpaying Chinese Association and chairman and committee member of the Shanghai French Concession Business General Association. Cheng Zhusong, 44 years old, from Songjiang, Jiangsu Province, is a former member of the Songjiang Municipal Council, the chairman of the Shanghai French Concession Business General Association, the chief of preparation for the Taxpaying Chinese Association, the chairman and committee member of the Provisional Council, and the owner of Zhu Hua Electric Knitting Factory. Jin Liren, 46 years old, from Wuxian, Jiangsu Province, was a tribute student during the Qing Dynasty and graduated from Meiji University in Japan.

Negotiations on the Submarine Cable Abolition Treaty

The Ministry of Communications insists on three specific principles, but the three companies have yet to respond.

Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable to be taken back tomorrow

The Ministry of Communications has finalized its plan for negotiations with the Great Eastern, Great Northern, and Pacific companies regarding the abolition of the submarine cable treaty. Representatives from the three companies have been formally requested to come to Beijing as soon as possible to continue discussions. Both sides are expected to adopt a sincere attitude and conclude a new contract within this year. Otherwise, since the old contract will expire at the end of this year, the Chinese government, to maintain its sovereignty, will have no choice but to declare the termination of all contractual relations with the companies. This reporter interviewed Wang Boqun, Minister of Communications, yesterday and inquired about this matter. He stated that the three companies have yet to respond since the ministry issued the letter.

Key issues in negotiation

Minister Wang also stated that the crux of the submarine cable treaty abolition negotiations lies in the following points. The three companies have already acknowledged abandoning the patent rights. What they are now contesting are: (1) the duration of landing rights, for which they are requesting twenty years; (2) the right to send and receive; and (3) the apportionment of electricity costs.

Specific principles

The specific principles that the Chinese side adheres to in the submarine cable negotiations are: (1) to strive to shorten the duration of landing rights; (2) the three companies are requesting the freedom to send and receive, but acknowledge China's right of supervision, while the Chinese side insists on having both the right to send and receive and the right of management; and (3) regarding the apportionment of electricity costs, the Chinese side insists that it should be equal to the apportionment methods stipulated in the contracts between those companies and other countries, and there should be no discrimination whatsoever.

Repurchase at assessed price

Minister Wang then stated that China has decided to repurchase the Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable at an assessed price, which is scheduled to be implemented on the 22nd of this month. Part of the price will be mortgaged to the banking sector with telecommunications public bonds, and another part will be allocated by the Remittance Bureau. Although five million yuan of telecommunications public bonds have been issued, they currently have no market value due to the lack of a solid fund, so they have to be temporarily mortgaged to the banking sector.

Zhenru Radio Station

When a reporter inquired about the progress of the Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations, he replied that the Sino-Japanese telecommunications negotiations opened in Beijing today (i.e., yesterday), and the results are not yet known. When asked when the Zhenru Radio Station will be able to communicate with France, Minister Wang replied that the construction, equipment, machinery, and other costs of the Zhenru Radio Station totaled more than two million yuan, and the results are quite good. Communication between China and France will be implemented in the near future. Next, communication between China and Britain will be carried out. The Fenglinqiao international branch station communicates with the Philippines, Hong Kong, and Java, but the various machinery and equipment of the radio station are not yet fully complete. It is estimated that an additional investment of one million yuan will be needed to achieve a large-scale operation. The Ministry of Communications is actively planning the progress of the construction, he said.

China National Aviation Corporation to Hold Board Meeting Today

To Discuss the Aftermath of the Accident

Wang Boqun's Talk to Reporters

Minister of Communications Wang Boqun arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 7:00 a.m. on the overnight express train from Beijing. Wang, who is the chairman of the board of directors of the China National Aviation Corporation, intends to convene a board meeting in Shanghai to discuss the responsibilities, compensation, and aftermath issues related to the crash of Shanghai Airplane No. 2. This reporter visited him yesterday and inquired in detail. The details of Mr. Wang's conversation are described below:

Board meeting

Wang stated that he has received a detailed report from the company regarding the plane crash. The board meeting is scheduled for 5:00 p.m. on the 21st (i.e., today) at the airline company. In addition to himself, the attendees will include Vice Minister Wei Yifu, Division Chief Liu Shufan, and American directors Poiin and Hamilton. The main scope of the meeting is to discuss various issues related to the aftermath. At that time, he also intends to summon the relevant personnel to inquire in detail about all the circumstances at that time for research.

Responsibility for the accident

Wang also stated that regarding the issue of responsibility for the accident, because the pilot and mechanical assistant of the Shanghai airplane have both died, there is no one to testify. Therefore, it is impossible to understand the circumstances of the flight and the airplane's machinery at that time. Moreover, the true cause of the accident cannot be explained. According to the company's report, the flight was quite low at the time, and it took off along the riverbank. The reason why it flew so low and along the riverbank was whether the airplane's machinery was damaged and it was necessary to land urgently on the river beach, or whether there were other reasons. So far, there is no evidence, so it can only be regarded as speculation and cannot be used as practical evidence.

Yang Yongtai's words

Wang continued, stating that all of these are factual difficulties. He went to the Baolong Hospital today (i.e., yesterday) to visit Mr. Yang Yongtai. Yang's spirits were quite good. He immediately asked about what happened at that time. According to him, Commander Xiong had fallen on top of him when the plane crashed. At that time, he felt quite uncomfortable and had difficulty breathing. He thought that the flight was too high and the air was thin, but he did not know that a major disaster had occurred. Yang was the least injured of the seven and was the most clear-headed at the time, and he was still confused. Moreover, he further stated that China does not have an aviation law, and even other countries lack it. Therefore, the issue of responsibility for the accident can only be handled with emotion rather than law. Regarding the issue of compensation for the dead and injured, Wang stated that the two pilots who died were company employees and should be given generous compensation. The compensation for the passengers should be submitted to the board of directors for further decision.

Shanghai-Yixing aviation

When asked when the Shanghai-Yixing aviation route will be opened, Wang replied that because the Shanghai airplane has crashed and there is a shortage of both airplanes and personnel, the expansion of the route has to be slowed down slightly. It is expected to be realized around January or February of next year. The Shanghai-Beijing route is still being planned. In the future, the company will carefully examine the driving talents and the airplane parts and components to ensure that they are foolproof. This matter should also be submitted to the board of directors for discussion and ways to rectify it, he said.
