U.S. Department of Agriculture Report on Cotton

The annual report of the U.S. Department of Agriculture on the cotton market states that it still emphasizes the importance of adjusting production to match demand. It also states that in recent years, there has been a trend of abandoning American cotton and using cotton from other countries. Price differences are unfavorable to American cotton, and quality differences are not as significant as before. This year's American cotton production is approximately 14.486 million bales, a decrease of 342,000 bales compared to 1929. This year's harvest can be considered sufficient to meet the reduced demand in the world market, with some surplus. The world's American cotton sales volume in 1929-1930 decreased by 2 million bales compared to the previous year, while the sales volume of Indian and other foreign cotton increased by 900,000 bales and 500,000 bales respectively. The decrease in the world's American cotton sales volume is partly due to the decrease in consumption by American cotton mills, and the remaining 1 million bales are equally divided between Continental Europe and England. Compared to the export volume in the previous year, exports to Germany decreased by 6%, exports to England decreased by 32%, and exports to Japan decreased by 21%. In the year ending June 30, 1930, the low level of American agricultural product exports was the lowest since 1915. The total value of exports this year was 14.95 million yuan, a decrease of 35.2 million yuan compared to the previous year. Although the decrease in exports is not limited to cotton, the decrease in value is largely due to the slow sales of American cotton and the lower average price.

Grain and Flour Market Remains Relatively Stable

Yesterday, the flour market was generally stable. This month, as the settlement date approaches, outside short sellers are considering covering their positions. Furthermore, sales of Tianjin flour have improved recently, and the demand for Shanghai flour has surged. High-quality brands such as "Battleship" and "Double Horse" are priced around 3.2 yuan, and Shanghai yuan is already at 3.22 yuan. As a result, the standard weight for this month has become tight again. Although the distant months were initially calm due to the slight increase in imported wheat, the market also tended to be firm as outside short sellers were eager to close their positions. However, after 3:00 PM, as foreign firms came to sell imported wheat at particularly low prices, factories again started to hedge, and market sentiment weakened again. As a result, this month was up 1.5%, January was up 5%, February was up 7.5%, March-May was up 2.5%, and April was unchanged compared to the previous day.

Recent Wheat Prices Suddenly Surge Before Settlement

Estimated Increase of 31 Points

Yesterday's futures market for the current month saw a sudden increase in tension, resulting in a rare squeeze situation. Because the short positions for this month were filled with expectations of previous months, it was thought that bullish investors would inevitably exit their positions. Unexpectedly, the bullish investors had already prepared to take delivery of the goods beforehand. As a result, general speculative short sellers had no goods at the time of settlement and had no choice but to lower their prices to sell. As a result, the market price gradually soared, and the highest closing price was as high as 4.63 yuan, an increase of 31 points compared to the previous closing price. Although buying and selling on the exchange is free, recklessly hoping for excessive gains without goods is seemingly self-inflicted. Distant months saw mixed gains and losses due to varying sentiment. January was up 4 points, February-March were slightly up 1 point, April was unchanged, and May was slightly down 2 points. There were no transactions for current wheat, but it is estimated that the imported wheat ordered by traders totaled 1,000 tons. Australian white wheat was sold at 2.55 yuan by Ren Cheng to the Wusong factory.

"Ke Xian" Rice Sales Active, Continuing to Rise by 20 Cents

Yesterday, there was not much "Ke Xian" rice arriving, and the local demand was even stronger. With limited arrivals and active sales, demand exceeded supply. As a result, the market was extremely active, and prices for all types of "Ke Xian" rice rose by 20 cents. If there is further inquiry from out-of-town merchants, market prices are expected to rise further. The overall market opened with Jiangxi machine-milled late rice at 11.8 yuan, Nanjing machine-milled rice at 10.019 yuan, Hunan rice at 10.03 yuan, Hunan machine-milled rice at 11.6 yuan, and Hunan oily rice at 11.5 yuan. Lower grades were priced accordingly. The market outlook remains positive.

Qing Feng's Garden

Green Clouds Under the Kerosene Lamp

When I am in the presence of all things that do not reveal themselves, the world is only the active radiance of my great kerosene lamp dancing childlike before my eyes. At this moment, I feel that if there were an electric lamp here, its motionless light would never be so lively. Thus, I feel that my kerosene lamp is as great as I am. Beside me is a tripod clock. I usually find it too clumsy, and it is too self-effacing in my house. But now, it really deserves your attention. How spirited it is! Each sound is more urgent than the last, each sound more solemn than the last. It is obviously not relaxing itself, expressing its strength and the spirit of our tense era with its tick-tock. Now its greatness is no less than that of my kerosene lamp. Thus, my position is shaken. I feel that there is a pair of formidable friends before me. I don't know if they have ever suffered setbacks or wounds in the past, but they are not tired at all! They are still in the brand-new age of youth. I suddenly realize, oh, how insignificant I am, how dejected I am. I am completely inferior to them. This should still be considered a genuine youth! I am only in my twenties, not even a few years older. Having experienced a bit of wind and frost and endured a bit of hardship in a surging era, isn't this precisely the sweet taste on a healthy life? What does this count for? Why let it become a scar on your heart?

Ten years of reading and working has only made me grow in worldly wisdom, and from worldly wisdom, it has only made me lose the courage to move forward, only made me hide in a corner with walls on both sides? Hovering on the boundary of society, being swayed by the winds and waves pushed out by the crowd, is this your original foothold? When you open the door of your room tomorrow and see the people you are close to, hear the laborious calls of the porters, see elementary school life running lively into the school, then think for yourself, where are you standing in this world, this great person after your quiet time?

This is a cigarette, and I am smoking again. But why smoke it? Is it because you are too tired and want to use it to relax your spirit? Do you still have important work to do and want to use it to boost your energy? Is it for the sake of the pungent taste? Then put it down. You hear the tick-tock sound, you see the flickering flame of the lamp, what are you doing?

Cigarette packs, peanut shells, scraps of paper, look, they are everywhere. Are they from yesterday or the day before? I understand very well that I have controlled myself today and have not eaten these things. This is certainly a good thing, right? Yes, of course, not eating peanuts for a day is naturally worthy of praise. But sweep it up, even the scraps of paper and cigarette butts. You haven't swept the floor for three days. Look, hasn't the lamplight already pointed it out to you in the corner?

Turning my eyes to the left, golden letters suddenly jumped into my eyes. (A collection of Shakespeare's plays), a friend I have known for more than three months. She is quiet but seems very angry, she is looking at me. That's right, she is annoyed. Although it has only been three months, it is too unfamiliar for her. I haven't even read a single piece.

Forget it, let's not be annoyed by anything. Tomorrow, the owner of this house will want to move.

Great Sea Market

Market News

The Double Wheel Toothbrush Company declares that this company was the first in our country to create machine-made toothbrushes, and for more than a decade, it has always taken promoting national products and resisting foreign powers as its mission. Although the sacrifices have been great over the years, we have spared no effort. Fortunately, we have been praised by people from all walks of life and are happy to use them. Now, for the convenience of customers' purchases, a special store has been set up at the east end of Shilu on Sanma Road, which will open soon. Retail sales of various toothbrushes of this brand and famous products from major national goods factories are also available. A special low price will be offered within three weeks of the opening to repay the kindness of all customers.

The Bai Luode Fountain Pen Company on North Sichuan Road declares that the technicians of our factory have recently researched and manufactured a unique fountain pen and double and single pen holder with new ideas. Since it first arrived at our company, it has been very popular with customers. Now, during the winter solstice discount period, the store is even more lively. It can be seen that people appreciate beauty, which is truly true.

The Shanghai Coca-Cola Company declares that at this time of advanced machinery, the machines used in this factory almost completely replace human labor. The entire process of manufacturing Coca-Cola and bottling is done entirely by machinery without any human contact. The most important step is the disinfection of the bottles. Once the bottles are disinfected, the drink can naturally remain pure. Two washers are used, placed at both ends of an extremely long circular belt. There are many small bags on the belt, and each bag holds one bottle. Jumping on one end of the washer, each jump causes the bottle to be turned upside down onto a single tube. This tube shoots a very strong caustic soda water upwards. This washing method is repeated as many as forty-two times. At the same time, the outside of the bottle is cleaned by a rotating brush. After this procedure, the mechanical movement transfers the bottles from the belt to the washer at the other end. This device has another row of tubes that emit clean, pure water to wash the inside and outside of the bottles. Every bottle must go through this disinfection procedure before it can be used to inject Coca-Cola.

The Asia-America Company declares that December 23 is the anniversary of the company's broadcasting station's first week of broadcasting. On this day, various materials, supplies, books, etc. will be specially discounted for one day, and the broadcasting program will be specially increased to entertain the audience. The broadcasting time for that day is listed below: 9:45 to 10:15, business news and old-fashioned records; 10:45 to 11:25, Shanghai Beach records; 12:15 to 12:40, short tune records; 1:00 to 1:30, four music records; 2:45 to 3:00, business news and Qinqiang records; 3:00 to 3:30, Kunqu records; 4:30 to 4:50, drum song records; 5:30 to 6:00, news 片 records; 6:00 to 6:20, Cantonese records; 6:30 to 7:25, storytelling; 7:35 to 8:30, storytelling; 8:30 to 8:45, song records; 8:45 to 9:45, special program, Shi Chunxuan Shanghai opera.

The Yimandeng Company at No. 9, Central House, No. 93 Sichuan Road, declares that the manager of this company has newly invented a platinum-decorated pocket stove that can keep warm for 24 hours. It is clean, elegant, lightweight, and exquisite, and the price is fair. There has been a large crowd of customers in the past few days.

The Xiang Sheng Trading Company declares that a new type of artistic New Year card has recently been discovered on the market. The style is extremely unique and the printing is very exquisite, which is very different from ordinary greeting cards on the market. The dozens of patterns are all pressed by machines. For example, the flower basket is completely pressed into a flower basket. The card is also equipped with a beautiful and exquisite calendar, so it can be hung on the wall or placed on the desk, which is both practical and has preservation value. It will surely be warmly welcomed by the recipient if it is given to relatives and friends. Compared with other greeting cards that are rigid in style and cannot be preserved, they are really incomparable. This new type of New Year card was invented by our company at No. 30, Caojia Street, West Gate, this port. Sincere, Wing On, New Sun and other companies, as well as World, Great Eastern, Qixin Civilization and other bookstores are selling them. The price is divided into two types, one dime and one dime two cents.

The China Gold Star Company declares that the newly invented pocket warmer is small in size, has a moderate temperature, and is very convenient to carry around. It is definitely an essential item for keeping out the cold, and it is far superior to imported products. The general wholesale office is attached to the Fuchangxiang Paint Shop in Fuyuli, Tiantang Street, French Concession, this port. Separate sales offices are located at Yingming Photo Studio at the intersection of Yingda Road and Wangping Street, and in major stores.

The Tao Tao Restaurant on Chongming Road, North Sichuan Road, declares that this restaurant was the first formal Guangzhou restaurant founded by Cantonese people in Shanghai. The dishes are specially prepared, the taste is excellent, and Shanghai people all know its reputation far and wide. Every evening, guests flock here. Ten years ago and now, a new branch has been opened at the former Anle site in Wuchang. It has been greatly renovated and redecorated. The halls are magnificent and the equipment is sophisticated. It took several months to set up before it opened on December 7th of the lunar calendar. Since its opening, the new hall's rooms have been reserved, and the seats for old customers are often full. Those who arrive later have almost no space in the new and old halls, and business is booming. The materials used are refined and clean, the cooking is delicious, the seating is elegant, and the service is attentive. I dare to inform those who like to eat Cantonese cuisine that Da Zhong and Da San Yuan are also branches of the same family, so the name is called Three Great Restaurants.

The Yonghua Department Store in West New Bridge declares that this company opened yesterday with a complete range of goods and low prices. The goods are excellent, and the customers are extremely enthusiastic. The store's sales were more than 45,000 yuan. In addition, the company's banking savings department also received more than 10,000 yuan in deposits, a new record that has never been seen in a store.
